# 增强对照表（源英文 → 加强英文 → 中文本地化）

> spec 共 37 个接口，1482 个对外字段/参数。逐字段对照「原文 → 加强 → 本地化」三态，判断改得更好还是更坏。

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_ai_keyword_data_keywords_search_volume_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides search volume data for your target keywords, reflecting their estimated usage in AI tools. | Returns estimated AI-tool search-volume data for the target keywords in a given location and language. | 查询 AI 关键词搜索量 keywords_search_volume_live |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field UTF-8 encoding The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000; The maximum number of characters in a single keyword: 250; The keywords will be converted to lowercase format;learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Target keywords whose AI search-volume data you want to retrieve. Each entry is processed as a separate keyword. | 需要查询 AI 搜索量的目标关键词，每个元素作为一个独立关键词处理。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don't specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/ai_keyword_data/locations_and_languages example: United Kingdom | Full location name (e.g. `United States`). Provide this or `location_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 完整的地理位置名称（如 `United States`）。与 `location_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.location_code` | unique location identifier required field if you don't specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/ai_keyword_data/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier. Provide this or `location_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 地理位置的数字标识。与 `location_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don't specify language_code if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/ai_keyword_data/locations_and_languages example: English | Full language name (e.g. `English`). Provide this or `language_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 完整的语言名称（如 `English`）。与 `language_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if you don't specify language_name if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/ai_keyword_data/locations_and_languages example: en | Language code (e.g. `en`). Provide this or `language_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 语言代码（如 `en`）。与 `language_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的地理位置代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的语言代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | number of results returned in the items array | Number of elements in this result's `items` array. | 该结果 `items` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains specified keywords with their AI search volume rates | The data records returned for this result. | 该结果返回的数据记录。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | specified keyword | The keyword this record refers to. | 该记录对应的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ai_search_volume` | current AI search volume rate of a keyword learn more about this metric here | Current AI search-volume rate for the keyword. | 该关键词当前的 AI 搜索量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ai_monthly_searches` | monthly AI search volume rates array of objects with AI search volume rates in a certain month of a year | Per-month AI search-volume history for the keyword. | 该关键词按月的 AI 搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ai_monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of the monthly data point. | 该月度数据点的年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ai_monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of the data point (1-12). | 该数据点的月份（1-12）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ai_monthly_searches.ai_search_volume` | AI search volume rate in a certain month of a year learn more about this metric here | AI search-volume rate for that month. | 该月的 AI 搜索量指标。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_chat_gpt_llm_responses_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live ChatGPT LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific ChatGPT AI model, based on the input parameters. | Returns a structured response from a chosen ChatGPT model for the given prompt and parameters, synchronously. | 实时获取 ChatGPT 模型响应 chat_gpt_llm_responses_live |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |
| `req.model_name` | name of the AI model required field model_nameconsists of the actual model name and version name; if the basic model name is specified, its latest version will be set by default; for example, if gpt-4.1 is specified, the gpt-4.1-2025-04-14 will be set as model_name automatically; you can receive the list of available LLM models by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/chat_gpt/llm_responses/models | Which AI model to query. Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |
| `req.max_output_tokens` | maximum number of tokens in the AI response optional field minimum value for reasoning models (e.g., reasoning is true in the Models endpoint): 1024; minimum value for non-reasoning models: 16; maximum value: 4096; default value: 2048 Note: if web_search is set to true or the reasoning model is specified in the request, the output token count may exceed the specified max_output_tokens limit | Upper bound on the number of tokens the model may generate in its reply. Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |
| `req.temperature` | randomness of the AI response optional field higher values make output more diverse; lower values make output more focused; minimum value: 0 maximum value: 2 default value: 0.94 Note: not supported in reasoning models | Sampling randomness: higher values make the output more varied, lower values make it more focused and deterministic. | 采样随机度：值越高输出越多样，值越低输出越聚焦、越确定。 |
| `req.top_p` |  | Nucleus-sampling threshold controlling response diversity by limiting which tokens are eligible for selection. | 核采样阈值，通过限制候选 token 的范围来控制响应的多样性。 |
| `req.web_search` | enable web search optional field when enabled, the AI model can access and cite current web information; default value: false; Note: refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support web_search; | Whether the model may access and cite current web information when answering. When disabled, the model answers from its training knowledge only. | 是否允许模型在作答时访问并引用实时网页信息；关闭时仅依据模型自身知识作答。 |
| `req.force_web_search` | force AI agent to use web search optional field to enable this parameter, web_search must also be enabled; when enabled, the AI model is forced to access and cite current web information; default value: false; Note: even if the parameter is set to true, there is no guarantee web sources will be cited in the response Note #2: not supported in reasoning models | Whether to force the model to perform a web search rather than leaving it optional. Requires web search to be enabled where that toggle exists. | 是否强制模型执行网页搜索（而非由模型自行决定）；在存在独立开关的接口中需先启用 web search。 |
| `req.web_search_country_iso_code` | ISO country code of the location optional field required if web_search_city is specified; to enable this parameter, web_search must also be enabled; when enabled, the AI model will search the web from the country you specify; Note: not supported in o3-mini, o1-pro, o1 models | ISO country code used to localize web-search results. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `req.web_search_city` | city name of the location optional field Note: specify web_search_country_iso_code to use this parameter Note #2: not supported in o3-mini, o1-pro, o1 models | City name used to localize web-search results. Requires `web_search_country_iso_code` to be set. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的城市名；需同时设置 `web_search_country_iso_code`。 |
| `req.system_message` | instructions for the AI behaviour optional field defines the AI's role, tone, or specific behavior you can specify up to 500 characters in the system_message field | Instructions that shape the AI's role, tone, or behavior, applied before the user prompt. | 用于设定 AI 角色、语气或行为的系统指令，先于用户提示生效。 |
| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain role and message parameters: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify the maximum of 10 message objects in the array; example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. | `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD includes the base task price plus the money_spent value | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.model_name` | name of the AI model used | Name of the AI model that produced the result. | 生成结果所用 AI 模型的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.input_tokens` | number of tokens in the input total count of tokens processed | Total number of tokens in the input. | 输入中的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.output_tokens` | number of tokens in the output total count of tokens generated in the AI response | Total number of tokens generated in the response. | 响应中生成的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.reasoning_tokens` | number of reasoning tokens total count of tokens used to generate reasoning content | Number of tokens used to produce the reasoning content. | 用于生成推理内容的 token 数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.web_search` | indicates if web search was used | Whether web search was used to produce this result. | 生成该结果是否使用了网页搜索。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.money_spent` | cost of AI tokens, USD the price charged by the third-party AI model provider for according to its Pricing | Amount charged by the third-party AI provider for the tokens, in USD. | 第三方 AI 提供方对本次 token 收取的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the result was produced, in UTC. | 结果生成的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | array of response items contains structured AI response data | The data records returned for this result. | 该结果返回的数据记录。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning` | element in the response | The reasoning element of the response (reasoning models only). | 响应中的推理元素（仅推理模型返回）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.type` | type of the element = 'reasoning' Note: this element is supported only in reasoning models and is not guaranteed to be returned | Element type marker for the reasoning element. | 推理元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections` | reasoning chain sections array of objects containing the reasoning chain sections generated by the LLM | The reasoning-chain sections generated by the model. | 模型生成的推理链分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections.type` | type of element='summary_text' | Element type marker for the reasoning section. | 推理分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections.text` | text of the reasoning chain section text of the reasoning chain section summarizing the model's thought process | Text summarizing this part of the model's thought process. | 概述模型该部分思考过程的文本。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message` | element in the response | The message element of the response. | 响应中的消息元素。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.type` | type of the element = 'message' | Element type marker for the message element. | 消息元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections` | array of content sections contains different parts of the AI response | The content sections that make up the AI message. | 构成 AI 消息的各内容分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.type` | type of element='text' | Element type marker for the content section. | 内容分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.text` | AI-generated text content | The AI-generated text content. | AI 生成的文本内容。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations` | array of references used to generate the response equals null if the web_search parameter is not set to true Note: annotations may return empty even when web_search is true, as the AI will attempt to retrieve web information but may not find relevant results | References cited to generate the response; null when web search was not used and may be empty. | 用于生成响应的引用来源；未使用网页搜索时为 null，也可能为空。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations.title` | the domain name or title of the quoted source | Domain name or title of the cited source. | 被引用来源的域名或标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations.url` | URL of the quoted source | URL of the cited source. | 被引用来源的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.fan_out_queries` | array of fan-out queries contains related search queries derived from the main query to provide a more comprehensive response | Related search queries derived from the main query to broaden the response. | 由主查询衍生、用于拓宽响应覆盖面的相关搜索查询。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_chat_gpt_llm_responses_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | ChatGPT LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific ChatGPT model, based on the input parameters. | Sets a ChatGPT LLM Responses task for later asynchronous collection via the Standard method. | 提交 ChatGPT 响应任务 chat_gpt_llm_responses_task_post |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |
| `req.model_name` | name of the AI model required field model_nameconsists of the actual model name and version name; if the basic model name is specified, its latest version will be set by default; for example, if gpt-4.1 is specified, the gpt-4.1-2025-04-14 will be set as model_name automatically; you can receive the list of available LLM models by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/chat_gpt/llm_responses/models | Which AI model to query. Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |
| `req.max_output_tokens` | maximum number of tokens in the AI response optional field minimum value for reasoning models (e.g., reasoning is true in the Models endpoint): 1024; minimum value for non-reasoning models: 16; maximum value: 4096; default value: 2048 | Upper bound on the number of tokens the model may generate in its reply. Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |
| `req.temperature` | randomness of the AI response optional field higher values make output more diverse; lower values make output more focused; minimum value: 0 maximum value: 2 default value: 0.94 Note: not supported in reasoning models | Sampling randomness: higher values make the output more varied, lower values make it more focused and deterministic. | 采样随机度：值越高输出越多样，值越低输出越聚焦、越确定。 |
| `req.top_p` |  | Nucleus-sampling threshold controlling response diversity by limiting which tokens are eligible for selection. | 核采样阈值，通过限制候选 token 的范围来控制响应的多样性。 |
| `req.system_message` | instructions for the AI behaviour optional field defines the AI's role, tone, or specific behavior; you can specify up to 500 characters in the system_message field | Instructions that shape the AI's role, tone, or behavior, applied before the user prompt. | 用于设定 AI 角色、语气或行为的系统指令，先于用户提示生效。 |
| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain role and message parameters: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify the maximum of 10 message objects in the array; example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special character in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL to which completed task results are POSTed (gzip-compressed). Use it to receive results via push instead of polling. | 任务完成后用于回推结果的 URL（结果以 gzip 压缩 POST 发送），可替代轮询主动接收结果。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special character in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL that receives a GET notification when the task completes, signaling that results are ready to collect. | 任务完成时收到 GET 通知的 URL，用于告知结果已可领取。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data array of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasksarray | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |

| `req.keyword` | keyword required field you can specify up to 2000 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |

Requires web search to be enabled where that toggle exists. | 是否强制模型执行网页搜索（而非由模型自行决定）；在存在独立开关的接口中需先启用 web search。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的地理位置代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的语言代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.model` | indicates the model version | The model version used. | 所使用的模型版本。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.check_url` | direct URL to search engine results you can use it to make sure that we provided exact results | Direct URL to the search results, usable to verify the returned data. | 直达搜索结果的 URL，可用于核对返回数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the result was produced, in UTC. | 结果生成的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.markdown` | content of the element in markdown format content of the result formatted in the markdown markup language | The result content rendered in Markdown. | 以 Markdown 渲染的结果内容。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_results` | array of search results all web search outputs the model retrieved when looking up information, including duplicates and unused entries | All web results the model retrieved while researching, including duplicates and unused entries. | 模型检索信息时获取的全部网页结果，含重复与未采用的条目。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.rating.rating_type` | type of rating here you can find the following elements: Max5, Percents, CustomMax | Scale of the rating, such as out of 5, percentage, or a custom maximum. | 评分采用的标度，如 5 分制、百分比或自定义上限。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.rating.value` | the average rating based on all reviews | Average rating across all reviews. | 所有评价的平均评分。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.rating.votes_count` | the number of votes | Number of votes behind the rating. | 构成该评分的投票数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.rating.rating_max` | the maximum value for a rating_type | Maximum possible value for the rating scale. | 该评分标度的最大可能值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.price` | product price | Product price. | 商品价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.currency` | currency of the listed price ISO code of the currency applied to the price | ISO currency code applied to the price. | 价格所用的 ISO 货币代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.tag` | tag text | Tag text shown on the product. | 商品上显示的标签文本。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.domain` | result domain in SERP | Domain of the product result. | 商品结果的域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.images` | image URLs of the element contains URLs leading to the images on the original resource or DataForSEO storage (in case the original source is not available) | Image URLs of the product, on the original source or DataForSEO storage if unavailable. | 商品的图片 URL，指向原始来源，或在不可用时指向 DataForSEO 存储。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids` | Google Shopping product identifiers array of Google Shopping product IDs associated with the product | Google Shopping product identifiers associated with this product. | 与该商品关联的 Google Shopping 商品标识集合。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.ei` | event identifier internal event identifier used by Google | Internal Google event identifier. | Google 内部事件标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.product_id` | product identifier can be used as a data_docid in Google Shopping API endpoints | Product identifier usable as `data_docid` in Google Shopping API endpoints. | 可作为 Google Shopping API 中 `data_docid` 使用的商品标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.catalog_id` | Google Shopping catalog identifier of the product can be used as a product_id in Google Shopping API endpoints | Google Shopping catalog identifier, usable as `product_id` in Google Shopping API endpoints. | Google Shopping 目录标识，可作为 Google Shopping API 中的 `product_id`。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.gpcid` | Google product cluster identifier can be used as a gid in Google Shopping API endpoints | Google product cluster identifier, usable as `gid` in Google Shopping API endpoints. | Google 商品聚类标识，可作为 Google Shopping API 中的 `gid`。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.headline_offer_docid` | document identifier of the main offer in the headline can be used as a data_docid in Google Shopping API endpoints | Document identifier of the headline offer, usable as `data_docid` in Google Shopping API endpoints. | 主推报价的文档标识，可作为 Google Shopping API 中的 `data_docid`。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.image_docid` | identifier for the displayed product’s image | Identifier of the displayed product image. | 所展示商品图片的标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.rds` | resource descriptor string internal Google resource descriptor string that identifies the product within Google's Shopping index | Internal Google resource descriptor string identifying the product in Google's Shopping index. | Google 内部资源描述符字符串，用于在 Google Shopping 索引中标识该商品。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.query` | search query search query used by ChatGPT to retrieve the product from Google Shopping | Search query ChatGPT used to retrieve the product from Google Shopping. | ChatGPT 用于从 Google Shopping 检索该商品的搜索查询。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.mid` | merchant identifier identifier of the seller or merchant account in Google Shopping | Identifier of the seller or merchant account in Google Shopping. | Google Shopping 中卖家或商家账户的标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.pvt` | product view type internal Google parameter that specifies the product view type used when rendering the product item | Internal Google parameter specifying the product view type used when rendering the item. | Google 内部参数，指定渲染商品条目时使用的展示类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.chat_gpt_products.items.product_ids.uule` | encoded location parameter indicates the location for a search | Encoded location parameter indicating the search location. | 编码的位置参数，表示搜索所用地点。 |

Requires web search to be enabled where that toggle exists. | 是否强制模型执行网页搜索（而非由模型自行决定）；在存在独立开关的接口中需先启用 web search。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_claude_llm_responses_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live Claude LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific Claude model, based on the input parameters. | Returns a structured response from a chosen Claude model for the given prompt and parameters, synchronously. | 实时获取 Claude 模型响应 claude_llm_responses_live |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |
| `req.model_name` | name of the AI model required field model_nameconsists of the actual model name and version name; if the basic model name is specified, its latest version will be set by default; for example, if claude-opus-4-0 is specified, the claude-opus-4-20250514 will be set as model_name automatically; you can receive the list of available LLM models by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/claude/llm_responses/models | Which AI model to query. Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |
| `req.max_output_tokens` | maximum number of tokens in the AI response optional field minimum value: 1; maximum value: 4096; default value: 2048; Note: if web_search is set to true or the reasoning model is specified in the request, the output token count may exceed the specified max_output_tokens limit Note #2: if use_reasoning is set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1025 | Upper bound on the number of tokens the model may generate in its reply. Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |
| `req.temperature` | randomness of the AI response optional field higher values make output more diverse; lower values make output more focused; minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1 default value: 0.7Note: temperature cannot be used together with top_p in the same request | Sampling randomness: higher values make the output more varied, lower values make it more focused and deterministic. | 采样随机度：值越高输出越多样，值越低输出越聚焦、越确定。 |
| `req.top_p` | diversity of the AI response optional field controls diversity of the response by limiting token selection; minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1 default value: nullNote: top_p cannot be used together with temperature in the same request | Nucleus-sampling threshold controlling response diversity by limiting which tokens are eligible for selection. | 核采样阈值，通过限制候选 token 的范围来控制响应的多样性。 |
| `req.web_search` | enable web search for current information optional field when enabled, the AI model can access and cite current web information; Note: refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support web_search; default value: false; The cost of the parameter can be calculated on the Pricing page | Whether the model may access and cite current web information when answering. When disabled, the model answers from its training knowledge only. | 是否允许模型在作答时访问并引用实时网页信息；关闭时仅依据模型自身知识作答。 |
| `req.force_web_search` | force AI agent to use web search optional field to enable this parameter, web_search must also be enabled; when enabled, the AI model is forced to access and cite current web information; default value: false; Note: even if the parameter is set to true, there is no guarantee web sources will be cited in the response | Whether to force the model to perform a web search rather than leaving it optional. Requires web search to be enabled where that toggle exists. | 是否强制模型执行网页搜索（而非由模型自行决定）；在存在独立开关的接口中需先启用 web search。 |
| `req.web_search_country_iso_code` | ISO country code of the location optional field possible values: 'AR','AT','AU','BE','BR','CA','CH','CL','CN','DE','DK','ES','FI','FR','GB','HK','ID','IN','IT','JP','KR','MX','MY','NL','NO','NZ','PH','PL','PT','RU','SA','SE','TR','TW','US','ZA' | ISO country code used to localize web-search results. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `req.web_search_city` | city name of the location optional field Note: specify web_search_country_iso_code to use this parameter | City name used to localize web-search results. Requires `web_search_country_iso_code` to be set. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的城市名；需同时设置 `web_search_country_iso_code`。 |
| `req.system_message` | instructions for the AI behaviour optional field defines the AI's role, tone, or specific behavior; you can specify up to 500 characters in the system_message field | Instructions that shape the AI's role, tone, or behavior, applied before the user prompt. | 用于设定 AI 角色、语气或行为的系统指令，先于用户提示生效。 |
| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain role and message parameters: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify the maximum of 10 message objects in the array; example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.use_reasoning` | enable reasoning for the AI model optional field when enabled, the model will perform reasoning before generating a response refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support reasoning default value: false Note: if set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1025 Note #2: if set to true, force_web_search must be set to false Note #3: if set to true, the temperature and top_p cannot be used | Whether the model should perform an explicit reasoning step before answering. Supported only by reasoning-capable models. | 是否让模型在作答前执行显式推理步骤，仅推理类模型支持。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |

Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.model_name` | name of the AI model used | Name of the AI model that produced the result. | 生成结果所用 AI 模型的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.input_tokens` | number of tokens in the input total count of tokens processed | Total number of tokens in the input. | 输入中的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.output_tokens` | number of tokens in the output total count of tokens generated in the AI response | Total number of tokens generated in the response. | 响应中生成的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.reasoning_tokens` | number of reasoning tokens total count of tokens used to generate reasoning content | Number of tokens used to produce the reasoning content. | 用于生成推理内容的 token 数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.web_search` | indicates if web search was used | Whether web search was used to produce this result. | 生成该结果是否使用了网页搜索。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.money_spent` | cost of AI tokens, USD the price charged by the third-party AI model provider for according to its Pricing | Amount charged by the third-party AI provider for the tokens, in USD. | 第三方 AI 提供方对本次 token 收取的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the result was produced, in UTC. | 结果生成的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | array of response items contains structured AI response data | The data records returned for this result. | 该结果返回的数据记录。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning` | element in the response | The reasoning element of the response (reasoning models only). | 响应中的推理元素（仅推理模型返回）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.type` | type of the element = 'reasoning' Note: this element is supported only in reasoning models and is not guaranteed to be returned | Element type marker for the reasoning element. | 推理元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections` | reasoning chain sections array of objects containing the reasoning chain sections generated by the LLM | The reasoning-chain sections generated by the model. | 模型生成的推理链分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections.type` | type of element='summary_text' | Element type marker for the reasoning section. | 推理分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections.text` | text of the reasoning chain section text of the reasoning chain section summarizing the model's thought process | Text summarizing this part of the model's thought process. | 概述模型该部分思考过程的文本。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message` | element in the response | The message element of the response. | 响应中的消息元素。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.type` | type of the element = 'message' | Element type marker for the message element. | 消息元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections` | array of content sections contains different parts of the AI response | The content sections that make up the AI message. | 构成 AI 消息的各内容分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.type` | type of element='text' | Element type marker for the content section. | 内容分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.text` | AI-generated text content | The AI-generated text content. | AI 生成的文本内容。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations` | array of references used to generate the response equals null if the web_search parameter is not set to true Note: annotations may return empty even when web_search is true, as the AI will attempt to retrieve web information but may not find relevant results | References cited to generate the response; null when web search was not used and may be empty. | 用于生成响应的引用来源；未使用网页搜索时为 null，也可能为空。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations.title` | the domain name or title of the quoted source | Domain name or title of the cited source. | 被引用来源的域名或标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations.url` | URL of the quoted source | URL of the cited source. | 被引用来源的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.fan_out_queries` | array of fan-out queries contains related search queries derived from the main query to provide a more comprehensive response | Related search queries derived from the main query to broaden the response. | 由主查询衍生、用于拓宽响应覆盖面的相关搜索查询。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_claude_llm_responses_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Claude LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific Claude model, based on the input parameters. | Sets a Claude LLM Responses task for later asynchronous collection via the Standard method. | 提交 Claude 响应任务 claude_llm_responses_task_post |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |
| `req.model_name` | name of the AI model required field model_nameconsists of the actual model name and version name; if the basic model name is specified, its latest version will be set by default; for example, if claude-opus-4-0 is specified, the claude-opus-4-20250514 will be set as model_name automatically; you can receive the list of available LLM models by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/claude/llm_responses/models | Which AI model to query. Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |
| `req.max_output_tokens` | maximum number of tokens in the AI response optional field minimum value: 1; maximum value: 4096; default value: 2048; Note: if web_search is set to true or the reasoning model is specified in the request, the output token count may exceed the specified max_output_tokens limit Note #2: if use_reasoning is set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1025 | Upper bound on the number of tokens the model may generate in its reply. Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |
| `req.temperature` | randomness of the AI response optional field higher values make output more diverse; lower values make output more focused; minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1 default value: 0.7Note: temperature cannot be used together with top_p in the same request | Sampling randomness: higher values make the output more varied, lower values make it more focused and deterministic. | 采样随机度：值越高输出越多样，值越低输出越聚焦、越确定。 |
| `req.top_p` | diversity of the AI response optional field controls diversity of the response by limiting token selection; minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1 default value: nullNote: top_p cannot be used together with temperature in the same request | Nucleus-sampling threshold controlling response diversity by limiting which tokens are eligible for selection. | 核采样阈值，通过限制候选 token 的范围来控制响应的多样性。 |
| `req.web_search` | enable web search for current information optional field when enabled, the AI model can access and cite current web information; Note: refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support web_search; default value: false; The cost of the parameter can be calculated on the Pricing page | Whether the model may access and cite current web information when answering. When disabled, the model answers from its training knowledge only. | 是否允许模型在作答时访问并引用实时网页信息；关闭时仅依据模型自身知识作答。 |
| `req.force_web_search` | force AI agent to use web search optional field to enable this parameter, web_search must also be enabled; when enabled, the AI model is forced to access and cite current web information; default value: false; Note: even if the parameter is set to true, there is no guarantee web sources will be cited in the response | Whether to force the model to perform a web search rather than leaving it optional. Requires web search to be enabled where that toggle exists. | 是否强制模型执行网页搜索（而非由模型自行决定）；在存在独立开关的接口中需先启用 web search。 |
| `req.web_search_country_iso_code` | ISO country code of the location optional field possible values: 'AR','AT','AU','BE','BR','CA','CH','CL','CN','DE','DK','ES','FI','FR','GB','HK','ID','IN','IT','JP','KR','MX','MY','NL','NO','NZ','PH','PL','PT','RU','SA','SE','TR','TW','US','ZA' | ISO country code used to localize web-search results. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `req.web_search_city` | city name of the location optional field Note: specify web_search_country_iso_code to use this parameter | City name used to localize web-search results. Requires `web_search_country_iso_code` to be set. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的城市名；需同时设置 `web_search_country_iso_code`。 |
| `req.system_message` | instructions for the AI behaviour optional field defines the AI's role, tone, or specific behavior; you can specify up to 500 characters in the system_message field | Instructions that shape the AI's role, tone, or behavior, applied before the user prompt. | 用于设定 AI 角色、语气或行为的系统指令，先于用户提示生效。 |
| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain role and message parameters: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify the maximum of 10 message objects in the array; example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.use_reasoning` | enable reasoning for the AI model optional field when enabled, the model will perform reasoning before generating a response refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support reasoning default value: false Note: if set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1025 Note #2: if set to true, force_web_search must be set to false Note #3: if set to true, the temperature and top_p cannot be used | Whether the model should perform an explicit reasoning step before answering. Supported only by reasoning-capable models. | 是否让模型在作答前执行显式推理步骤，仅推理类模型支持。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special character in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL to which completed task results are POSTed (gzip-compressed). Use it to receive results via push instead of polling. | 任务完成后用于回推结果的 URL（结果以 gzip 压缩 POST 发送），可替代轮询主动接收结果。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special character in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL that receives a GET notification when the task completes, signaling that results are ready to collect. | 任务完成时收到 GET 通知的 URL，用于告知结果已可领取。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasksarray | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | unique task identifier in our system unique task identifier in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Results of the task; null at this stage, collect them later via the task id. | 任务结果；此阶段为 null，请稍后凭任务 id 领取。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_gemini_llm_responses_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live Gemini LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific Gemini AI model, based on the input parameters. | Returns a structured response from a chosen Gemini model for the given prompt and parameters, synchronously. | 实时获取 Gemini 模型响应 gemini_llm_responses_live |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |
| `req.model_name` | name of the AI model required field model_nameconsists of the actual model name and version name; if the basic model name is specified, its latest version will be set by default; for example, if gemini-1.5-pro is specified, the gemini-1.5-pro-002 will be set as model_name automatically; you can receive the list of available LLM models by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/gemini/llm_responses/models | Which AI model to query. Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |
| `req.max_output_tokens` | maximum number of tokens in the AI response optional field minimum value: 1 maximum value: 4096; default value: 2048; Note: if web_search is set to true or the reasoning model is specified in the request, the output token count may exceed the specified max_output_tokens limit Note #2: if use_reasoning is set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1024 | Upper bound on the number of tokens the model may generate in its reply. Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |
| `req.temperature` | randomness of the AI response optional field higher values make output more diverse lower values make output more focused minimum value: 0 maximum value: 2 default value: 1.3 | Sampling randomness: higher values make the output more varied, lower values make it more focused and deterministic. | 采样随机度：值越高输出越多样，值越低输出越聚焦、越确定。 |
| `req.top_p` | diversity of the AI response optional field controls diversity of the response by limiting token selection minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1 default value: 0.9 | Nucleus-sampling threshold controlling response diversity by limiting which tokens are eligible for selection. | 核采样阈值，通过限制候选 token 的范围来控制响应的多样性。 |
| `req.web_search` | enable web search for current information optional field when enabled, the AI model can access and cite current web information; Note: refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support web_search; default value: false; The cost of the parameter can be calculated on the Pricing page | Whether the model may access and cite current web information when answering. When disabled, the model answers from its training knowledge only. | 是否允许模型在作答时访问并引用实时网页信息；关闭时仅依据模型自身知识作答。 |
| `req.system_message` | instructions for the AI behavior optional field defines the AI's role, tone, or specific behavior you can specify up to 500 characters in the system_message field | Instructions that shape the AI's role, tone, or behavior, applied before the user prompt. | 用于设定 AI 角色、语气或行为的系统指令，先于用户提示生效。 |
| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain role and message parameters: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify the maximum of 10 message objects in the array; example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.use_reasoning` | enable reasoning for the AI model optional field when enabled, the model will perform reasoning before generating a response refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support reasoning default value: false Note: if set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1024 Note #2: for Gemini Pro models, the use_reasoning will automatically be set to true | Whether the model should perform an explicit reasoning step before answering. Supported only by reasoning-capable models. | 是否让模型在作答前执行显式推理步骤，仅推理类模型支持。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD includes the base task price plus the money_spent value | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.model_name` | name of the AI model used | Name of the AI model that produced the result. | 生成结果所用 AI 模型的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.input_tokens` | number of tokens in the input total count of tokens processed | Total number of tokens in the input. | 输入中的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.output_tokens` | number of tokens in the output total count of tokens generated in the AI response | Total number of tokens generated in the response. | 响应中生成的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.reasoning_tokens` | number of reasoning tokens total count of tokens used to generate reasoning content | Number of tokens used to produce the reasoning content. | 用于生成推理内容的 token 数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.web_search` | indicates if web search was used | Whether web search was used to produce this result. | 生成该结果是否使用了网页搜索。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.money_spent` | cost of AI tokens, USD the price charged by the third-party AI model provider for according to its Pricing | Amount charged by the third-party AI provider for the tokens, in USD. | 第三方 AI 提供方对本次 token 收取的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the result was produced, in UTC. | 结果生成的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | array of response items contains structured AI response data | The data records returned for this result. | 该结果返回的数据记录。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning` | element in the response | The reasoning element of the response (reasoning models only). | 响应中的推理元素（仅推理模型返回）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.type` | type of the element = 'reasoning' Note: this element is supported only in reasoning models and is not guaranteed to be returned | Element type marker for the reasoning element. | 推理元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections` | reasoning chain sections array of objects containing the reasoning chain sections generated by the LLM | The reasoning-chain sections generated by the model. | 模型生成的推理链分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections.type` | type of element='summary_text' | Element type marker for the reasoning section. | 推理分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.reasoning.sections.text` | text of the reasoning chain section text of the reasoning chain section summarizing the model's thought process | Text summarizing this part of the model's thought process. | 概述模型该部分思考过程的文本。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message` | element in the response | The message element of the response. | 响应中的消息元素。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.type` | type of the element = 'message' | Element type marker for the message element. | 消息元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections` | array of content sections contains different parts of the AI response | The content sections that make up the AI message. | 构成 AI 消息的各内容分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.type` | type of element='text' | Element type marker for the content section. | 内容分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.text` | AI-generated text content | The AI-generated text content. | AI 生成的文本内容。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations` | array of references used to generate the response equals null if the web_search parameter is not set to true Note: annotations may return empty even when web_search is true, as the AI will attempt to retrieve web information but may not find relevant results | References cited to generate the response; null when web search was not used and may be empty. | 用于生成响应的引用来源；未使用网页搜索时为 null，也可能为空。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations.title` | the domain name or title of the quoted source | Domain name or title of the cited source. | 被引用来源的域名或标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.message.sections.annotations.url` | redirect URL to the quoted source contains a Vertex AI redirect that leads to the original source | URL of the cited source. | 被引用来源的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.fan_out_queries` | array of fan-out queries contains related search queries derived from the main query to provide a more comprehensive response | Related search queries derived from the main query to broaden the response. | 由主查询衍生、用于拓宽响应覆盖面的相关搜索查询。 |

| `resp.200.result.reasoning` | indicates if the AI model supports reasoning | Whether this model supports reasoning. | 该模型是否支持推理。 |
| `resp.200.result.web_search_supported` | web search support for the AI model if true, the web_search parameter can be set with the AI model | Whether web search can be enabled for this model. | 该模型是否可启用网页搜索。 |
| `resp.200.result.task_post_supported` | indicates if Standard (POST-GET) data retrieval is supported if true, you can use the Standard (POST-GET) data retrieval method with the AI model | Whether this model supports the Standard (POST-then-GET) retrieval method. | 该模型是否支持标准（先 POST 后 GET）的取数方式。 |

## get_dataforseo_ai_optimization_gemini_llm_responses_task_get_id

| `(operation)` | Gemini LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific Gemini model, based on the input parameters. | Retrieves the results of a previously set Gemini LLM Responses task by its id. | 按 id 获取 Gemini 响应结果 gemini_llm_responses_task_get_id |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | The task id you requested results for; valid for 30 days. | 你所查询结果的任务 id，有效期 30 天。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_gemini_llm_responses_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Gemini LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific Gemini model, based on the input parameters. | Sets a Gemini LLM Responses task for later asynchronous collection via the Standard method. | 提交 Gemini 响应任务 gemini_llm_responses_task_post |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |

Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |

Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |

| `req.web_search` | enable web search for current information optional field when enabled, the AI model can access and cite current web information; Note: refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support web_search; default value: false; The cost of the parameter can be calculated on the Pricing page | Whether the model may access and cite current web information when answering. When disabled, the model answers from its training knowledge only. | 是否允许模型在作答时访问并引用实时网页信息；关闭时仅依据模型自身知识作答。 |

| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain role and message parameters: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify the maximum of 10 message objects in the array; example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.use_reasoning` | enable reasoning for the AI model optional field when enabled, the model will perform reasoning before generating a response refer to the Models endpoint for a list of models that support reasoning default value: false Note: if set to true, the minimum value for max_output_tokens is 1024 Note #2: for Gemini Pro models, the use_reasoning will automatically be set to true | Whether the model should perform an explicit reasoning step before answering. Supported only by reasoning-capable models. | 是否让模型在作答前执行显式推理步骤，仅推理类模型支持。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special character in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL to which completed task results are POSTed (gzip-compressed). Use it to receive results via push instead of polling. | 任务完成后用于回推结果的 URL（结果以 gzip 压缩 POST 发送），可替代轮询主动接收结果。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special character in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL that receives a GET notification when the task completes, signaling that results are ready to collect. | 任务完成时收到 GET 通知的 URL，用于告知结果已可领取。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |

Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Results of the task; null at this stage, collect them later via the task id. | 任务结果；此阶段为 null，请稍后凭任务 id 领取。 |

| `(operation)` | Live Gemini LLM Scraper endpoint provides structured results from Gemini. The results are specific to the selected location (see [the List of Locations](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/gemini/llm_scraper/locations.md)), language (see [the List of Languages](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/gemini/llm_scraper/languages.md)), and keyword. | Returns structured Gemini results for a keyword, localized by location and language, synchronously. | 实时抓取 Gemini 结构化结果 gemini_llm_scraper_live_advanced |
| `req.keyword` | keyword required field you can specify up to 2000 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.gemini_images.items.image_url` | URL of the image the URL leading to the image on the original resource or DataForSEO storage (in case the original source is not available) | URL of the image itself, on the original source or on DataForSEO storage if the source is unavailable. | 图片本身的 URL，指向原始来源，或在原始来源不可用时指向 DataForSEO 存储。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.gemini_images.items.markdown` | content of the element in markdown format content of the result formatted in the markdown markup language | The image item rendered in Markdown. | 以 Markdown 渲染的图片条目。 |

We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23learn more on our Help Center | URL to which completed task results are POSTed (gzip-compressed). Use it to receive results via push instead of polling. | 任务完成后用于回推结果的 URL（结果以 gzip 压缩 POST 发送），可替代轮询主动接收结果。 |

## get_dataforseo_ai_optimization_gemini_llm_scraper_tasks_ready

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | The **‘Tasks Ready’** endpoint is designed to provide you with the list of completed tasks, which haven’t been collected yet. If you use the Standard method without specifying the `postback_url`, you can receive the list of `id` for all completed tasks using this endpoint. Then, you can collect the results using the **‘Task GET’** endpoint. | Lists completed Gemini LLM Scraper tasks that have not yet been collected. | 获取已完成的 Gemini 抓取任务 gemini_llm_scraper_tasks_ready |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |

| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the parameters passed in the request's URL | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.result` | array of results | Results produced by this request. | 本次请求产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.result.id` | task identifier of the completed task unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Identifier of the completed task, in UUID format. | 已完成任务的标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.result.se` | search engine specified when setting the task | The search engine specified when the task was set. | 设置任务时指定的搜索引擎。 |
| `resp.200.result.function` | search engine function example: llm_scraper | The search-engine function of the task (e.g. `llm_scraper`). | 任务的搜索引擎功能（如 `llm_scraper`）。 |
| `resp.200.result.date_posted` | date when the task was posted (in the UTC format) | When the task was submitted, in UTC. | 任务提交的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.result.tag` | user-defined task identifier | Your own label supplied when the task was set. | 设置任务时你自定义的标签。 |
| `resp.200.result.endpoint_advanced` | URL for collecting the results of the Advanced task if the Advanced function is not supported in the specified endpoint, the value will be null | URL to collect the Advanced results of the task; null when Advanced is unsupported. | 领取该任务 Advanced 结果的 URL；不支持 Advanced 时为 null。 |
