## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_llm_mentions_aggregated_metrics_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live LLM Mentions endpoint provides aggregated metrics for mentions of the keywords or domains specified in the `target` array of the request. The results are specific to the selected platform (`google` for Google’s AI Overview or `chat_gpt` for ChatGPT), location and language parameters (see [the List of Locations & Languages](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages.md)). | Returns aggregated LLM-mention metrics for the target keywords or domains, grouped along several dimensions. | 实时获取 LLM 提及聚合指标 llm_mentions_aggregated_metrics_live |
| `req.target` | array of objects containing target entities required field you can specify up to 10 entities (objects) in the target field one target entity can contain either one domain or one keyword and related parametersexamples: target array with a domain entity [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}] target array with a keyword entity [{"keyword": "bmw", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"}] target array with multiple entities [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}, {"keyword": "bmw", "match_type ": "partial_match", "search_scope": ["answer"]}] | The entities to analyze. Each element is a domain entity or keyword entity describing what to track in LLM mentions. | 要分析的目标实体集合，每个元素为描述待追踪对象的域名实体或关键词实体。 |
| `req.domain_entity` | domain entity in the target array example: {"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude", "search_scope": ["sources"]} | A target specified as a domain, with its own search filter and scope. | 以域名形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤与范围设置。 |
| `req.domain` | target domain required field if you don't specify keyword you can specify up to 63 characters in the domain field; a domain should be specified without https:// and www. | The target domain to track. Provide this or `keyword` within the entity. | 要追踪的目标域名，与实体内的 `keyword` 二选一。 |
| `req.search_filter` | target keyword search filter optional field possible values: include, exclude default value: include | Whether matches for this target are included in or excluded from the analysis. | 该目标的命中结果是纳入还是排除于分析。 |
| `req.search_scope` | target keyword search scope optional field possible values: any, question, answer, brand_entities, fan_out_queries default value: any | Which parts of the LLM interaction to search for the target, such as the question, answer, brand entities, or fan-out queries. | 在 LLM 交互的哪些部分中搜索该目标，如问题、回答、品牌实体或扩展查询等。 |
| `req.include_subdomains` | indicates if the subdomains of the target domain will be included in the search optional field if set to true, the subdomains will be included in the search default value: false | Whether subdomains of the target domain are counted as matches. | 是否将目标域名的子域名计为命中。 |
| `req.keyword_entity` | keyword entity in the target array example: {"keyword": "bmw", "search_filter": "include", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"} | A target specified as a keyword, with its own search filter, scope, and match type. | 以关键词形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤、范围与匹配方式设置。 |
| `req.keyword` | target keyword required field if you don't specify domain you can specify up to 250 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |
| `req.match_type` | target keyword match type optional field word_match - full-text search for terms that match the specified seed keyword with additional words included before, after, or within the key phrase (e.g., search for “light” will return results with “light bulb”, “light switch”); partial_match - substring search that finds all instances containing the specified sequence of characters, even if it appears inside a longer word (e.g., search for “light” will return results with “lighting”, “highlight”); possible values: word_match, partial_match default value: word_match | How the keyword is matched against text: word-level full-text matching or partial matching. | 关键词与文本的匹配方式：按词的全文匹配或部分匹配。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search location optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_code if you don't specify this field, the location_code with 2840 value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for United States only | Full location name (e.g. `United States`). Provide this or `location_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 完整的地理位置名称（如 `United States`）。与 `location_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.location_code` | search location code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: 2840 Note: chat_gpt data is available for 2840 only | Numeric location identifier. Provide this or `location_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 地理位置的数字标识。与 `location_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search language optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_code; if you don't specify this field, the language_code with en value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for English only | Full language name (e.g. `English`). Provide this or `language_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 完整的语言名称（如 `English`）。与 `language_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_code` | search language code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_name; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code_by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: en Note: chat_gpt data is available for en onlyn | Language code (e.g. `en`). Provide this or `language_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 语言代码（如 `en`）。与 `language_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.platform` | target platform optional field possible values: chat_gpt, google default value: google Note: the data returned depends on the selected platform Note #2:chat_gpt data is available for the United States and English only | Which AI platform the data is drawn from. The returned data depends on the selected platform. | 数据来源的 AI 平台，返回数据随所选平台而不同。 |
| `req.initial_dataset_filters` | array of filter expressions applied before aggregation optional field you can use this array to filter expressions applied to the raw mentions database before aggregation to limit the rows contributing to the result;you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: =, , in, not_in, like, not_like, ilike, not_ilike, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["ai_search_volume",">","1000"]the full list of possible filters is available here. learn more about the initial dataset filters in this help center article. | Filter expressions applied to the raw mentions data before aggregation. | 在聚合之前对原始 mentions 数据应用的过滤表达式。 |
| `req.internal_list_limit` | maximum number of elements within internal arrays optional field you can use this field to limit the number of elements within the following arrays: sources_domain search_results_domain minimum value: 1 maximum value: 20 default value: 10 | Caps the number of elements returned within each nested array in the result. | 限制结果中每个内嵌数组返回的元素数量。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.brand_entities_category.mentions` | total LLM mentions count the number of times the target keyword or domain were mentioned in relation to the specific domain | Number of times the target keyword or domain was mentioned for this grouping key. | 目标关键词或域名在该分组键下被提及的次数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.brand_entities_category.ai_search_volume` | current AI search volume rate of a keyword learn more about this metric here | Current AI search-volume rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 搜索量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.brand_entities_category.impressions` | current AI impressions rate of a keyword | Current AI impressions rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 曝光量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | individual pages results array containing detailed mention metrics for each of the found top pages in this case, equals null | Per-page detail records; null for this aggregated-metrics endpoint. | 逐页面明细记录；该聚合指标接口下为 null。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_llm_mentions_cross_aggregated_metrics_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live LLM Mentions endpoint provides aggregated metrics grouped by custom keys for mentions of the keywords or domains specified in the `target` array of the request. Each item in the results array corresponds to the specified target. The results are specific to the selected platform (`google` for Google’s AI Overview or `chat_gpt` for ChatGPT), location and language parameters (see [the List of Locations & Languages](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages.md)). | Returns aggregated LLM-mention metrics grouped by custom aggregation keys, for comparing multiple target sets. | 实时对比多组 LLM 提及聚合指标 llm_mentions_cross_aggregated_metrics_live |
| `req.targets` | array of objects containing target entities with aggregation keys required field you can specify up to 10, but not less than 2 target sets of parameters, each with its aggregation_key;example of a targets array with multiple entities: [{"aggregation_key":"bmw","target":[{"domain":"en.wikipedia.org","search_filter":"exclude"},{"keyword":"m5","match_type":"partial_match","search_scope":["answer"]}]},{"aggregation_key":"mercedes","target":[{"domain":"www.mercedes-benz.com","search_filter":"exclude"},{"keyword":"GLC","match_type":"word_match"}]}] | Sets of target entities to compare. Each set carries its own aggregation key so results can be grouped side by side. | 用于对比的多组目标实体，每组带各自的聚合键，便于结果分组并列展示。 |
| `req.aggregation_key` | aggregation key for grouping the results required field groups results for comparison and serves as a label for the group; you can specify up to 250 characters in the aggregation_key field | Label identifying a target set; results are grouped and compared under this key. | 标识某一组目标的聚合键，结果按该键分组并对比。 |
| `req.target` | array of objects containing target entities required field a single target can contain up to 10 domain and/or keyword entities | The entities to analyze. Each element is a domain entity or keyword entity describing what to track in LLM mentions. | 要分析的目标实体集合，每个元素为描述待追踪对象的域名实体或关键词实体。 |
| `req.domain_entity` | domain entity in the target array example: {"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude", "search_scope": ["sources"]} | A target specified as a domain, with its own search filter and scope. | 以域名形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤与范围设置。 |
| `req.domain` | target domain required field if you don't specify a keyword you can specify up to 63 characters in the domain field; a domain should be specified without https:// and www. | The target domain to track. Provide this or `keyword` within the entity. | 要追踪的目标域名，与实体内的 `keyword` 二选一。 |
| `req.search_filter` | target keyword search filter optional field possible values: include, exclude default value: include | Whether matches for this target are included in or excluded from the analysis. | 该目标的命中结果是纳入还是排除于分析。 |
| `req.search_scope` | target keyword search scope optional field possible values: any, question, answer, brand_entities, fan_out_queries default value: any | Which parts of the LLM interaction to search for the target, such as the question, answer, brand entities, or fan-out queries. | 在 LLM 交互的哪些部分中搜索该目标，如问题、回答、品牌实体或扩展查询等。 |
| `req.include_subdomains` | indicates if the subdomains of the target domain will be included in the search optional field if set to true, the subdomains will be included in the search default value: false | Whether subdomains of the target domain are counted as matches. | 是否将目标域名的子域名计为命中。 |
| `req.keyword_entity` | keyword entity in the target array example: {"keyword": "bmw", "search_filter": "include", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"} | A target specified as a keyword, with its own search filter, scope, and match type. | 以关键词形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤、范围与匹配方式设置。 |
| `req.keyword` | target keyword required field if you don't specify a domain you can specify up to 250 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |
| `req.match_type` | target keyword match type defines how the specified keyword is matched optional field possible values: word_match - full-text search for terms that match the specified seed keyword with additional words included before, after, or within the key phrase (e.g., search for "light" will return results with "light bulb", "light switch"); partial_match - substring search that finds all instances containing the specified sequence of characters, even if it appears inside a longer word (e.g., search for "light" will return results with "lighting", "highlight"); default value: word_match | How the keyword is matched against text: word-level full-text matching or partial matching. | 关键词与文本的匹配方式：按词的全文匹配或部分匹配。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search location optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_code if you don't specify this field, the location_code with 2840 value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for United States only | Full location name (e.g. `United States`). Provide this or `location_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 完整的地理位置名称（如 `United States`）。与 `location_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.location_code` | search location code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: 2840 Note: chat_gpt data is available for 2840 only | Numeric location identifier. Provide this or `location_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 地理位置的数字标识。与 `location_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search language optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_code; if you don't specify this field, the language_code with en value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for English only | Full language name (e.g. `English`). Provide this or `language_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 完整的语言名称（如 `English`）。与 `language_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_code` | search language code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_name; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code_by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: en Note: chat_gpt data is available for en onlyn | Language code (e.g. `en`). Provide this or `language_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 语言代码（如 `en`）。与 `language_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.platform` | target platform optional field possible values: chat_gpt, google default value: google Note: the data returned depends on the selected platform Note #2:chat_gpt data is available for the United States and English only | Which AI platform the data is drawn from. The returned data depends on the selected platform. | 数据来源的 AI 平台，返回数据随所选平台而不同。 |
| `req.initial_dataset_filters` | array of filter expressions applied before aggregation optional field you can use this array to filter expressions applied to the raw mentions database before aggregation to limit the rows contributing to the result;you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: =, , in, not_in, like, not_like, ilike, not_ilike, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["ai_search_volume",">","1000"]the full list of possible filters is available here. learn more about the initial dataset filters in this help center article. | Filter expressions applied to the raw mentions data before aggregation. | 在聚合之前对原始 mentions 数据应用的过滤表达式。 |
| `req.internal_list_limit` | maximum number of elements within internal arrays optional field you can use this field to limit the number of elements within the following arrays: sources_domain search_results_domain minimum value: 1 maximum value: 10 default value: 5 | Caps the number of elements returned within each nested array in the result. | 限制结果中每个内嵌数组返回的元素数量。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |

| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.language.mentions` | total LLM mentions count the number of times the target keyword or domain were mentioned in relation to this specific grouping key | Number of times the target keyword or domain was mentioned for this grouping key. | 目标关键词或域名在该分组键下被提及的次数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.language.ai_search_volume` | current AI search volume rate of a keyword learn more about this metric here | Current AI search-volume rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 搜索量指标。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_llm_mentions_search_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live LLM Mentions Search endpoint provides mention data and related metrics from AI searches. The results are specific to the selected platform (`google` for Google’s AI Overview or `chat_gpt` for ChatGPT), as well as location and language parameters (see [the List of Locations & Languages](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages.md)). | Returns mention records and related metrics from AI searches for the target keywords or domains. | 实时搜索 LLM 提及数据 llm_mentions_search_live |
| `req.target` | array of objects containing target entities required field you can specify up to 10 entities (objects) in the target field one target entity can contain either one domain or one keyword and related parametersexamples: target array with a domain entity [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}] target array with a keyword entity [{"keyword": "bmw", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"}] target array with multiple entities [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}, {"keyword": "bmw", "match_type ": "partial_match", "search_scope": ["answer"]}] | The entities to analyze. Each element is a domain entity or keyword entity describing what to track in LLM mentions. | 要分析的目标实体集合，每个元素为描述待追踪对象的域名实体或关键词实体。 |
| `req.domain_entity` | domain entity in the target array example: {"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude", "search_scope": ["sources"]} | A target specified as a domain, with its own search filter and scope. | 以域名形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤与范围设置。 |
| `req.domain` | target domain required field if you don't specify keyword you can specify up to 63 characters in the domain field; a domain should be specified without https:// and www. | The target domain to track. Provide this or `keyword` within the entity. | 要追踪的目标域名，与实体内的 `keyword` 二选一。 |
| `req.search_filter` | target keyword search filter optional field possible values: include, exclude default value: include | Whether matches for this target are included in or excluded from the analysis. | 该目标的命中结果是纳入还是排除于分析。 |
| `req.search_scope` | target keyword search scope optional field possible values: any, question, answer, brand_entities, fan_out_queries default value: any | Which parts of the LLM interaction to search for the target, such as the question, answer, brand entities, or fan-out queries. | 在 LLM 交互的哪些部分中搜索该目标，如问题、回答、品牌实体或扩展查询等。 |
| `req.include_subdomains` | indicates if the subdomains of the target domain will be included in the search optional field if set to true, the subdomains will be included in the search default value: false | Whether subdomains of the target domain are counted as matches. | 是否将目标域名的子域名计为命中。 |
| `req.keyword_entity` | keyword entity in the target array example: {"keyword": "bmw", "search_filter": "include", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"} | A target specified as a keyword, with its own search filter, scope, and match type. | 以关键词形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤、范围与匹配方式设置。 |
| `req.keyword` | target keyword required field if you don't specify domain you can specify up to 250 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |
| `req.match_type` | target keyword match type defines how the specified keyword is matched optional field possible values: word_match - full-text search for terms that match the specified seed keyword with additional words included before, after, or within the key phrase (e.g., search for "light" will return results with "light bulb", "light switch"); partial_match - substring search that finds all instances containing the specified sequence of characters, even if it appears inside a longer word (e.g., search for "light" will return results with "lighting", "highlight"); default value: word_match | How the keyword is matched against text: word-level full-text matching or partial matching. | 关键词与文本的匹配方式：按词的全文匹配或部分匹配。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search location optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_code if you don't specify this field, the location_code with 2840 value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for United States only | Full location name (e.g. `United States`). Provide this or `location_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 完整的地理位置名称（如 `United States`）。与 `location_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.location_code` | search location code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: 2840 Note: chat_gpt data is available for 2840 only | Numeric location identifier. Provide this or `location_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 地理位置的数字标识。与 `location_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search language optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_code; if you don't specify this field, the language_code with en value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for English only | Full language name (e.g. `English`). Provide this or `language_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 完整的语言名称（如 `English`）。与 `language_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_code` | search language code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_name; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code_by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: en Note: chat_gpt data is available for en onlyn | Language code (e.g. `en`). Provide this or `language_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 语言代码（如 `en`）。与 `language_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.platform` | target platform optional field possible values: chat_gpt, google default value: google Note: the data returned depends on the selected platform Note #2:chat_gpt data is available for the United States and English only | Which AI platform the data is drawn from. The returned data depends on the selected platform. | 数据来源的 AI 平台，返回数据随所选平台而不同。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: =, , in, not_in, like, not_like, ilike, not_ilike, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["ai_search_volume",">","1000"]The full list of possible filters is available here. | Filtering rules applied to the returned results. Multiple filters can be combined with logical operators. | 应用于返回结果的过滤规则，可用逻辑运算符组合多个过滤条件。 |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results possible sorting types: asc - results will be sorted in the ascending order desc - results will be sorted in the descending order you should use a comma to set up a sorting type example: ["ai_search_volume,desc"] note that you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules | Sorting rules for the returned results, using ascending or descending order on selected fields. | 返回结果的排序规则，按选定字段升序或降序排列。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of the returned mentions data optional fielddefault value: 0 example: if you specify the 10 value, the first ten mentions objects in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive objects; Note: the maximum value is 9,000, use the search_after_token if you would like to offset more results | Number of leading results to skip in the returned array, used for paging. | 返回数组中跳过的起始结果数，用于分页。 |
| `req.search_after_token` | token for subsequent requests optional field provided in the identical filed of the response to each request; use this parameter to avoid timeouts while trying to obtain over 20,000 results in a single request; by specifying the unique search_after_token value from the response array, you will get the subsequent results of the initial task; search_after_token values are unique for each subsequent task ; Note: if the search_after_token is specified in the request, all other parameters should be identical to the previous request | Cursor token from a previous response; pass it to fetch the next batch of results without time-window limits. | 上一次响应返回的游标令牌，传入后可获取下一批结果且不受时间窗口限制。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of returned objects optional fielddefault value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Maximum number of objects to return. | 返回对象的最大数量。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results relevant the request | Total number of results matching the request. | 匹配请求的结果总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.current_offset` | the number of mentions objects that are omitted in the items array | Number of mention objects skipped before the returned `items`. | 返回的 `items` 之前被跳过的提及对象数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_after_token` | token for subsequent requests by specifying the unique search_after_token when setting a new task, you will get the subsequent results of the initial task; search_after_token values are unique for each subsequent task | Cursor token to pass in a subsequent request to fetch the next batch of results. | 游标令牌，在后续请求中传入以获取下一批结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of elements in this result's `items` array. | 该结果 `items` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains relevant mentions data | The matching mention records. | 匹配的提及记录。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.platform` | platform received in a POST array | Platform echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的平台。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.model_name` | name of the AI model from which the data was retrieved Note: for the google platform type, the value is always google_ai_overview | Name of the AI model the data was retrieved from. | 数据来源的 AI 模型名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的地理位置代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request. | 回显请求中的语言代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.question` | relevant question | The question associated with this mention. | 与该提及关联的问题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.answer` | relevant answer in markdown format content of the result formatted in the markdown markup language | The relevant answer, rendered in Markdown. | 以 Markdown 渲染的相关回答。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources` | array of sources the sources the model cited or relied on in its final answer | The sources the model cited or relied on in its final answer. | 模型在最终回答中引用或依据的来源。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.snippet` | source description | Description snippet of the source. | 来源的描述摘要。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.source_name` | source name | Name of the source. | 来源名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.thumbnail` | source thumbnail | Thumbnail image of the source. | 来源缩略图。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.markdown` | content of the element in markdown format content of the result formatted in the markdown markup language | The source content rendered in Markdown. | 以 Markdown 渲染的来源内容。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.position` | position in the results | Position of the source in the results. | 来源在结果中的位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.title` | source title | Title of the source. | 来源标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.domain` | source domain | Domain of the source. | 来源域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.url` | source URL | URL of the source. | 来源 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sources.publication_date` | date and time when the result was published in the format: “year-month-date:minutes:UTC_difference_hours:UTC_difference_minutes” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the source was published. | 来源的发布时间。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results` | array of search results all web search outputs the model retrieved when looking up information, including duplicates and unused entries | All web results the model retrieved while researching, including duplicates and unused entries. | 模型检索信息时获取的全部网页结果，含重复与未采用的条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.description` | result description | Description snippet of the search result. | 搜索结果的描述摘要。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.breadcrumb` | breadcrumb | Breadcrumb path of the search result. | 搜索结果的面包屑路径。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.position` | position in the results | Position of the search result. | 搜索结果的位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.title` | result title | Title of the search result. | 搜索结果的标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.domain` | result domain | Domain of the search result. | 搜索结果的域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.url` | result URL | URL of the search result. | 搜索结果的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_results.publication_date` | date and time when the result was published in the format: “year-month-date:minutes:UTC_difference_hours:UTC_difference_minutes” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the search result was published. | 搜索结果的发布时间。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ai_search_volume` | current AI search volume rate of a keyword learn more about this metric here | Current AI search-volume rate for the keyword. | 该关键词当前的 AI 搜索量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches` | monthly AI search volume rates array of objects with AI search volume rates in a certain month of a year | Per-month AI search-volume history for the keyword. | 该关键词按月的 AI 搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of the monthly data point. | 该月度数据点的年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of the data point (1-12). | 该数据点的月份（1-12）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.search_volume` | AI search volume rate in a certain month of a year learn more about this metric here | AI search-volume rate for that month. | 该月的 AI 搜索量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.first_response_at` | date and time when the response data was first recorded in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2025-10-21 06:25:30 +00:00 | When the response data was first recorded, in UTC. | 响应数据首次被记录的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.last_response_at` | date and time when the response data was last updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2025-10-21 06:25:30 +00:00 | When the response data was last updated, in UTC. | 响应数据最近一次更新的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities` | array of brand entities contains information on brands mentioned in the response | Brands mentioned in the response. | 响应中提及的品牌。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities.position` | position in the results | Position of the brand in the results. | 品牌在结果中的位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities.title` | name of the brand | Brand name. | 品牌名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities.category` | category of the brand | Brand category. | 品牌类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.fan_out_queries` | array of fan-out queries contains related search queries derived from the main query to provide a more comprehensive response | Related search queries derived from the main query to broaden the response. | 由主查询衍生、用于拓宽响应覆盖面的相关搜索查询。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_llm_mentions_top_domains_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live LLM Mentions Top Domains endpoint provides aggregated LLM mentions metrics grouped by the most frequently mentioned domains for the specified `target`. The results are specific to the selected platform (`google` for Google’s AI Overview or `chat_gpt` for ChatGPT), location and language parameters (see [the List of Locations & Languages](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages.md)). | Returns aggregated LLM-mention metrics grouped by the most frequently mentioned domains for the target. | 实时获取 LLM 提及热门域名 llm_mentions_top_domains_live |
| `req.target` | array of objects containing target entities required field you can specify up to 10 entities (objects) in the target field one target entity can contain either one domain or one keyword and related parametersexamples: target array with a domain entity [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}] target array with a keyword entity [{"keyword": "bmw", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"}] target array with multiple entities [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}, {"keyword": "bmw", "match_type ": "partial_match", "search_scope": ["answer"]}] | The entities to analyze. Each element is a domain entity or keyword entity describing what to track in LLM mentions. | 要分析的目标实体集合，每个元素为描述待追踪对象的域名实体或关键词实体。 |
| `req.domain_entity` | domain entity in the target array example: {"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude", "search_scope": ["sources"]} | A target specified as a domain, with its own search filter and scope. | 以域名形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤与范围设置。 |
| `req.domain` | target domain required field if you don't specify keyword you can specify up to 63 characters in the domain field; a domain should be specified without https:// and www. | The target domain to track. Provide this or `keyword` within the entity. | 要追踪的目标域名，与实体内的 `keyword` 二选一。 |
| `req.search_filter` | target keyword search filter optional field possible values: include, exclude default value: include | Whether matches for this target are included in or excluded from the analysis. | 该目标的命中结果是纳入还是排除于分析。 |
| `req.search_scope` | target keyword search scope optional field possible values: any, question, answer, brand_entities, fan_out_queries default value: any | Which parts of the LLM interaction to search for the target, such as the question, answer, brand entities, or fan-out queries. | 在 LLM 交互的哪些部分中搜索该目标，如问题、回答、品牌实体或扩展查询等。 |
| `req.include_subdomains` | indicates if the subdomains of the target domain will be included in the search optional field if set to true, the subdomains will be included in the search default value: false | Whether subdomains of the target domain are counted as matches. | 是否将目标域名的子域名计为命中。 |
| `req.keyword_entity` | keyword entity in the target array example: {"keyword": "bmw", "search_filter": "include", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"} | A target specified as a keyword, with its own search filter, scope, and match type. | 以关键词形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤、范围与匹配方式设置。 |
| `req.keyword` | target keyword required field if you don't specify domain you can specify up to 250 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |
| `req.match_type` | target keyword match type optional field possible values: word_match, partial_match word_match - full-text search for terms that match the specified seed keyword with additional words included before, after, or within the seed key phrase. partial_match - searches for any occurrence of the keyword or its parts within the content default value: word_match | How the keyword is matched against text: word-level full-text matching or partial matching. | 关键词与文本的匹配方式：按词的全文匹配或部分匹配。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search location optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_code if you don't specify this field, the location_code with 2840 value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for United States only | Full location name (e.g. `United States`). Provide this or `location_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 完整的地理位置名称（如 `United States`）。与 `location_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.location_code` | search location code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: 2840 Note: chat_gpt data is available for 2840 only | Numeric location identifier. Provide this or `location_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 地理位置的数字标识。与 `location_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search language optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_code; if you don't specify this field, the language_code with en value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for English only | Full language name (e.g. `English`). Provide this or `language_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 完整的语言名称（如 `English`）。与 `language_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_code` | search language code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_name; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code_by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: en Note: chat_gpt data is available for en onlyn | Language code (e.g. `en`). Provide this or `language_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 语言代码（如 `en`）。与 `language_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.platform` | target platform optional field possible values: chat_gpt, google default value: google Note: the data returned depends on the selected platform Note #2:chat_gpt data is available for the United States and English only | Which AI platform the data is drawn from. The returned data depends on the selected platform. | 数据来源的 AI 平台，返回数据随所选平台而不同。 |
| `req.links_scope` | links source scope optional field this parameter specifies which links will be used to extract domains and aggregation data possible values: sources, search_results default value: sources | Which links are used to extract domains/pages and their aggregation data. | 用于提取域名/页面及其聚合数据的链接范围。 |
| `req.initial_dataset_filters` | array of filter expressions applied before aggregation optional field you can use this array to filter expressions applied to the raw mentions database before aggregation to limit the rows contributing to the result;you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: =, , in, not_in, like, not_like, ilike, not_ilike, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["ai_search_volume",">","1000"]the full list of possible filters is available here. learn more about the initial dataset filters in this help center article. | Filter expressions applied to the raw mentions data before aggregation. | 在聚合之前对原始 mentions 数据应用的过滤表达式。 |
| `req.items_list_limit` | maximum number of results in the items array optional field you can use this parameter to limit the number of data objects you receive in the items array minimum value: 1 maximum value: 10 default value: 5 | Caps the number of objects returned in the top-level `items` array. | 限制顶层 `items` 数组返回的对象数量。 |
| `req.internal_list_limit` | maximum number of elements within internal arrays optional field you can use this field to limit the number of elements within the following arrays: sources_domain search_results_domain minimum value: 1 maximum value: 10 default value: 5 | Caps the number of elements returned within each nested array in the result. | 限制结果中每个内嵌数组返回的元素数量。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |

Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.total` | aggregated mentions metrics summary contains overall aggregated LLM mention metrics across all found domains, grouped by various dimensions | Overall aggregated LLM-mention metrics for the target, grouped along several dimensions. | 针对目标的整体 LLM 提及聚合指标，按多个维度分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.location` | location-based grouping array of objects containing mention metrics segmented by geographical location | Mention metrics for location-based grouping. | 按地理位置分组的提及指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.location.type` | type of the element = 'group_element' | Element type marker for the group element. | 分组元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.location.key` | grouping identifier the specific identifier for the grouping dimension | Identifier of this grouping bucket (e.g. the location, language, or domain name). | 该分组桶的标识（如地理位置、语言或域名）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.location.mentions` | total LLM mentions count the number of times the target keyword or domain were mentioned in relation to this specific grouping key | Number of times the target keyword or domain was mentioned for this grouping key. | 目标关键词或域名在该分组键下被提及的次数。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_llm_mentions_top_pages_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live LLM Mentions Top Pages endpoint provides aggregated LLM mentions metrics grouped by the most frequently mentioned pages for the specified `target`. The results are specific to the selected platform (`google` for Google’s AI Overview or `chat_gpt` for ChatGPT), location and language parameters (see [the List of Locations & Languages](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages.md)). | Returns aggregated LLM-mention metrics grouped by the most frequently mentioned pages for the target. | 实时获取 LLM 提及热门页面 llm_mentions_top_pages_live |
| `req.target` | array of objects containing target entities required field you can specify up to 10 entities (objects) in the target field one target entity can contain either one domain or one keyword and related parametersexamples: target array with a domain entity [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}] target array with a keyword entity [{"keyword": "bmw", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"}] target array with multiple entities [{"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude"}, {"keyword": "bmw", "match_type ": "partial_match", "search_scope": ["answer"]}] | The entities to analyze. Each element is a domain entity or keyword entity describing what to track in LLM mentions. | 要分析的目标实体集合，每个元素为描述待追踪对象的域名实体或关键词实体。 |
| `req.domain_entity` | domain entity in the target array example: {"domain": "en.wikipedia.org", "search_filter": "exclude", "search_scope": ["sources"]} | A target specified as a domain, with its own search filter and scope. | 以域名形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤与范围设置。 |
| `req.domain` | target domain required field if you don't specify keyword you can specify up to 63 characters in the domain field; a domain should be specified without https:// and www. | The target domain to track. Provide this or `keyword` within the entity. | 要追踪的目标域名，与实体内的 `keyword` 二选一。 |
| `req.search_filter` | target keyword search filter optional field possible values: include, exclude default value: include | Whether matches for this target are included in or excluded from the analysis. | 该目标的命中结果是纳入还是排除于分析。 |
| `req.search_scope` | target keyword search scope optional field possible values: any, question, answer, brand_entities, fan_out_queries default value: any | Which parts of the LLM interaction to search for the target, such as the question, answer, brand entities, or fan-out queries. | 在 LLM 交互的哪些部分中搜索该目标，如问题、回答、品牌实体或扩展查询等。 |
| `req.include_subdomains` | indicates if the subdomains of the target domain will be included in the search optional field if set to true, the subdomains will be included in the search default value: false | Whether subdomains of the target domain are counted as matches. | 是否将目标域名的子域名计为命中。 |
| `req.keyword_entity` | keyword entity in the target array example: {"keyword": "bmw", "search_filter": "include", "search_scope": ["question"], "match_type ": "partial_match"} | A target specified as a keyword, with its own search filter, scope, and match type. | 以关键词形式指定的目标，带有自己的搜索过滤、范围与匹配方式设置。 |
| `req.keyword` | target keyword required field if you don't specify domain you can specify up to 250 characters in the keyword field all %## will be decoded (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) if you need to use the “%” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%25”; if you need to use the “+” character for your keyword, please specify it as “%2B”learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | The single search term to look up. | 用于查询的单个搜索词。 |
| `req.match_type` | target keyword match type optional field possible values: word_match, partial_match word_match - full-text search for terms that match the specified seed keyword with additional words included before, after, or within the seed key phrase. partial_match - searches for any occurrence of the keyword or its parts within the content default value: word_match | How the keyword is matched against text: word-level full-text matching or partial matching. | 关键词与文本的匹配方式：按词的全文匹配或部分匹配。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search location optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_code if you don't specify this field, the location_code with 2840 value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for United States only | Full location name (e.g. `United States`). Provide this or `location_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 完整的地理位置名称（如 `United States`）。与 `location_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.location_code` | search location code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: 2840 Note: chat_gpt data is available for 2840 only | Numeric location identifier. Provide this or `location_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Locations endpoint. | 地理位置的数字标识。与 `location_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Locations 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search language optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_code; if you don't specify this field, the language_code with en value will be used by default; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages Note: chat_gpt data is available for English only | Full language name (e.g. `English`). Provide this or `language_code`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 完整的语言名称（如 `English`）。与 `language_code` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.language_code` | search language code optional field if you use this field, you don't need to specify language_name; you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code_by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/llm_mentions/locations_and_languages default value: en Note: chat_gpt data is available for en onlyn | Language code (e.g. `en`). Provide this or `language_name`; the available values come from the corresponding Languages endpoint. | 语言代码（如 `en`）。与 `language_name` 二选一，可选值见对应的 Languages 列表接口。 |
| `req.platform` | target platform optional field possible values: chat_gpt, google default value: google Note: the data returned depends on the selected platform Note #2:chat_gpt data is available for the United States and English only | Which AI platform the data is drawn from. The returned data depends on the selected platform. | 数据来源的 AI 平台，返回数据随所选平台而不同。 |
| `req.links_scope` | links source scope optional field this parameter specifies which links will be used to extract pages and aggregation data possible values: sources, search_results default value: sources | Which links are used to extract domains/pages and their aggregation data. | 用于提取域名/页面及其聚合数据的链接范围。 |
| `req.initial_dataset_filters` | array of filter expressions applied before aggregation optional field you can use this array to filter expressions applied to the raw mentions database before aggregation to limit the rows contributing to the result;you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: =, , in, not_in, like, not_like, ilike, not_ilike, match, not_match you can use the % operator with like and not_like to match any string of zero or more characters example: ["ai_search_volume",">","1000"]the full list of possible filters is available here. learn more about the initial dataset filters in this help center article. | Filter expressions applied to the raw mentions data before aggregation. | 在聚合之前对原始 mentions 数据应用的过滤表达式。 |
| `req.items_list_limit` | maximum number of results in the items array optional field you can use this parameter to limit the number of data objects you receive in the items array minimum value: 1 maximum value: 10 default value: 5 | Caps the number of objects returned in the top-level `items` array. | 限制顶层 `items` 数组返回的对象数量。 |
| `req.internal_list_limit` | maximum number of elements within internal arrays optional field you can use this field to limit the number of elements within the following arrays: sources_domain search_results_domain minimum value: 1 maximum value: 10 default value: 5 | Caps the number of elements returned within each nested array in the result. | 限制结果中每个内嵌数组返回的元素数量。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total` | aggregated mentions metrics summary contains overall aggregated LLM mention metrics across all found top pages, grouped by various dimensions | Overall aggregated LLM-mention metrics for the target, grouped along several dimensions. | 针对目标的整体 LLM 提及聚合指标，按多个维度分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.location` | location-based grouping array of objects containing mention metrics segmented by geographical location | Mention metrics for location-based grouping. | 按地理位置分组的提及指标。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.total.location.key` | grouping identifier the specific identifier for the grouping dimension | Identifier of this grouping bucket (e.g. the location, language, or domain name). | 该分组桶的标识（如地理位置、语言或域名）。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_title.ai_search_volume` | current AI search volume rate of a keyword learn more about this metric here | Current AI search-volume rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 搜索量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_title.impressions` | current AI impressions rate of a keyword | Current AI impressions rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 曝光量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_category` | data on brand entities relevant to the target array of objects containing data on brand entity categories that appear in search results related to LLM queries | Mention metrics for brand-entity categories appearing in results. | 结果中出现的品牌实体类别的提及指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_category.type` | type of the element = 'group_element' | Element type marker for the group element. | 分组元素的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_category.key` | grouping identifier the specific identifier for the grouping dimension in this case the field displays a found brand entity category | Identifier of this grouping bucket (e.g. the location, language, or domain name). | 该分组桶的标识（如地理位置、语言或域名）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_category.mentions` | total LLM mentions count the number of times the target keyword or domain were mentioned in relation to the specific domain | Number of times the target keyword or domain was mentioned for this grouping key. | 目标关键词或域名在该分组键下被提及的次数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_category.ai_search_volume` | current AI search volume rate of a keyword learn more about this metric here | Current AI search-volume rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 搜索量指标。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.brand_entities_category.impressions` | current AI impressions rate of a keyword | Current AI impressions rate for the keyword in this grouping. | 该分组下关键词当前的 AI 曝光量指标。 |

## post_dataforseo_ai_optimization_perplexity_llm_responses_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Live Perplexity LLM Responses endpoint allows you to retrieve structured responses from a specific Perplexity AI model, based on the input parameters. | Returns a structured response from a chosen Perplexity model for the given prompt and parameters, synchronously. | 实时获取 Perplexity 模型响应 perplexity_llm_responses_live |
| `req.user_prompt` | prompt for the AI model required field the question or task you want to send to the AI model; you can specify up to 500 characters in the user_prompt field | The question or instruction sent to the AI model. | 发送给 AI 模型的问题或指令。 |
| `req.model_name` | name of the AI model required field model_nameconsists of the actual model name and version name; if the basic model name is specified, its latest version will be set by default; you can receive the list of available LLM models by making a separate request to the following endpoint: https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/ai_optimization/perplexity/llm_responses/models | Which AI model to query. Combines the base model name and version; the available values come from the corresponding Models endpoint. | 指定要调用的 AI 模型，由基础模型名与版本组成，可选值见对应的 Models 列表接口。 |
| `req.max_output_tokens` | maximum number of tokens in the AI response optional field minimum value: 1 maximum value: 4096; default value: 2048; Note: if the reasoning model is specified in the request, the output token count may exceed the specified max_output_tokens limit | Upper bound on the number of tokens the model may generate in its reply. Limits response length and cost. | 模型回复可生成的最大 token 数，用于限制响应长度与成本。 |
| `req.temperature` | randomness of the AI response optional field higher values make output more diverse lower values make output more focused minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1.9 default value: 0.77 | Sampling randomness: higher values make the output more varied, lower values make it more focused and deterministic. | 采样随机度：值越高输出越多样，值越低输出越聚焦、越确定。 |
| `req.top_p` | diversity of the AI response optional field controls diversity of the response by limiting token selection minimum value: 0 maximum value: 1 default value: 0.9 | Nucleus-sampling threshold controlling response diversity by limiting which tokens are eligible for selection. | 核采样阈值，通过限制候选 token 的范围来控制响应的多样性。 |
| `req.web_search_country_iso_code` | country code for web search localization optional field specify the country ISO code to get localized web search results Note: available only for Perplexity Sonar models example: US | ISO country code used to localize web-search results. | 用于本地化网页搜索结果的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `req.system_message` | instructions for the AI behavior optional field defines the AI's role, tone, or specific behavior you can specify up to 500 characters in the system_message field | Instructions that shape the AI's role, tone, or behavior, applied before the user prompt. | 用于设定 AI 角色、语气或行为的系统指令，先于用户提示生效。 |
| `req.message_chain` | conversation history optional field array of message objects representing previous conversation turns; each object must contain: role string with either user or ai role; message string with message content (max 500 characters); you can specify maximum of 10 message objects in the array; Note: for Perplexity models, messages must strictly alternate between user and AI roles (user → ai); example: "message_chain": [{"role":"user","message":"Hello, what’s up?"},{"role":"ai","message":"Hello! I’m doing well, thank you. How can I assist you today?"}] | Prior conversation turns supplied as context. Each element is a message object carrying a role and its content. | 作为上下文传入的历史对话轮次，每个元素是带 role 与内容的消息对象。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can match results to requests. | 你自定义的任务标签，会在响应中原样返回，便于将结果与请求对应。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | The API version that produced this response. | 生成本次响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code of the response. Inspect it to detect request-level errors. | 本次响应的总体状态码，用于判断请求级别的错误。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Total execution time of the request, in seconds. | 请求的总执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total cost of all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本次响应中所有任务的总费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array. | `tasks` 数组中的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the `tasks` array that returned an error. | `tasks` 数组中返回错误的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of tasks created for this request. | 为本次请求创建的任务列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务的唯一标识，UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Status code of this individual task. Use it to tell whether the task itself succeeded. | 该任务自身的状态码，用于判断单个任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Execution time of this task, in seconds. | 该任务的执行时间（秒）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD includes the base task price plus the money_spent value | Cost of this task, in USD. | 该任务的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's `result` array. | 该任务 `result` 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | API route segments of the endpoint that handled this task. | 处理该任务的接口路由分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Results produced by this task. | 该任务产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.model_name` | name of the AI model used | Name of the AI model that produced the result. | 生成结果所用 AI 模型的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.input_tokens` | number of tokens in the input total count of tokens processed | Total number of tokens in the input. | 输入中的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.output_tokens` | number of tokens in the output total count of tokens generated in the AI response | Total number of tokens generated in the response. | 响应中生成的 token 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.web_search` | indicates if web search was used Note: web search is enabled by default in Perplexity Sonar models | Whether web search was used to produce this result. | 生成该结果是否使用了网页搜索。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.money_spent` | cost of AI tokens, USD the price charged by the third-party AI model provider for according to its Pricing | Amount charged by the third-party AI provider for the tokens, in USD. | 第三方 AI 提供方对本次 token 收取的费用（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When the result was produced, in UTC. | 结果生成的时间（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | array of response items contains structured AI response data | The data records returned for this result. | 该结果返回的数据记录。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.type` | type of the element = 'message' | Element type marker for the response item. | 响应条目的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sections` | array of content sections contains different parts of the AI response | The content sections that make up the AI message. | 构成 AI 消息的各内容分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sections.type` | type of element='text' | Element type marker for the content section. | 内容分段的类型标记。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sections.text` | AI-generated text content | The AI-generated text content. | AI 生成的文本内容。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sections.annotations` | array of references used to generate the response equals null if the web_search parameter is not set to true Note: annotations may return empty even when web_search is true, as the AI will attempt to retrieve web information but may not find relevant results | References cited to generate the response; null when web search was not used and may be empty. | 用于生成响应的引用来源；未使用网页搜索时为 null，也可能为空。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sections.annotations.title` | the domain name or title of the quoted source | Domain name or title of the cited source. | 被引用来源的域名或标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.sections.annotations.url` | URL of the quoted source | URL of the cited source. | 被引用来源的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.fan_out_queries` | array of fan-out queries contains related search queries derived from the main query to provide a more comprehensive response | Related search queries derived from the main query to broaden the response. | 由主查询衍生、用于拓宽响应覆盖面的相关搜索查询。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status. | 该任务状态的可读说明信息。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the parameters passed in the URL of the GET request | Echo of the parameters you supplied for this task. | 回显你为该任务提交的参数。 |
| `resp.200.result` | array of results | Results produced by this request. | 本次请求产生的结果。 |
| `resp.200.result.model_name` | name of the AI model | Name of the available AI model. | 可用 AI 模型的名称。 |
| `resp.200.result.reasoning` | indicates if the AI model supports reasoning | Whether this model supports reasoning. | 该模型是否支持推理。 |
| `resp.200.result.web_search_supported` | web search support for the AI model if true, the web_search parameter can be set with the AI model | Whether web search can be enabled for this model. | 该模型是否可启用网页搜索。 |
| `resp.200.result.task_post_supported` | indicates if Standard (POST-GET) data retrieval is supported if true, you can use the Standard (POST-GET) data retrieval method with the AI model | Whether this model supports the Standard (POST-then-GET) retrieval method. | 该模型是否支持标准（先 POST 后 GET）的取数方式。 |
